Richard Washington, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, Electric Pirates Holdings, Inc. (richie@blackbeard.com), 32 years old, New York City, USA
Greetings to Santa fans and believers worldwide! I'm Richard
Washington, Founder, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of
Electric Pirates Entertainment. Like you who have discovered
this very special site, I have a special fondness for Santa
Claus and his deeds and works. Over a decade ago, the father-
and-son production team of Alexander and Ilya Salkind gave the
world their own incredible vision of the Merriest Man on Earth.
When I saw that film --- "Santa Claus: The Movie" --- in 1985,
not only was my life changed as a result, but I soon became,
and indeed remain, one of Santa's most loyal elves. In spirit,
of course. The Santa Claus of Greenland Foundation did itself
mighty proud indeed last year, when the 1995 Santa Summit was
given its own place here on the Internet; and let me tell you,
I'm very much looking forward to seeing Jorgen Rosland defend
his title as Santa Games World Champion this year. To those
who will be part of the 1996 Santa Summit, all of us at EPE
wish you the best of luck as you represent your country. We
know that the tasks ahead of you will be very much similar
to those faced by the 17 Santas who participated in last
year's Summit. To you who represent the Foundation, my thanks
for your having conceived and developed this site. Please
continue to have it up for as long as there's an Internet.
Finally, to the Man himself: For the last 11 years, I have
continually pushed myself over the line for you. The road has
always been tough, but you and I share a common bond, dear
Santa: we perservere because we've got enthusiasm, passion,
love, adventurous spirit --- and, most importantly of all,
what we New Yorkers call chutzpah! I look forward to using
the above ingredients in making possible my further adventures
with you. From the Electric Pirates Family to Santa Claus
believers throughout the world: Merry Christmas! 'Nuff said.

finn peter hansen (B.248), 17 years old, 3932.ARSUK GREENLAND

Kære Julemand
Det er koldt i Danmark nu og alt tyder på en hvid jul. Mine julegave-ønsker bliver opfyldt, det ved jeg ligesom alle de øvrige ting, jeg har brudt mit hoved med i 1996 vil blive klaret her inden jul.
Da jeg engang spillede julemand for nogle børn i en børnehave lærte jeg julemandens magi at kende. Nemlig den sære sindsstemning der rammer en, når man har fået tøjet på og børnene kigger forventningsfuldt på en. Så er man ikke bare klædt ud som julemanden. Man ER julemanden.
Så julemanden findes i os alle - ingen tvivl om det.

God jul - måske kommer vi og besøger dig i april 1997 sammen med et kamerahold.

\Martin

Merry Christmas

This is not my story, thus, who ever did the investigation will remain
untold.

As a result of an overwhelming lack of requests, and with research help
from tget renown scientific journal SPY magazine (January, 1990)
- I am pleased to present the annual scientific inquiry into Santa Clause.

1. No known species of reindeer can fly. BUT there are 300.000 species of
living organisms yet to be classified, and while most of these are insects
and germs, this does not COMPLETELY rule out flying reindeer.

c 'fly'
2. There are 2 billion children (persons under 18) in the world BUT since
Santa doesn't (appear) to handle the Muslim , Hindu, Jewish and Buddhist
children, that reduces the workload to 15% of the total 378 million
according to the Population Reference Bureau, equals average rate of 3.5
children per household, thats 91.8 million homes. One presumes there's at
least one good child in each home.

3. Santa has 31 hours of work to do, due to the rotation of earth. This

results in 822.6 visits per second. Which actually means that Santa has
1\1000th of a second to park, hop out of the sleigh, jump down the chimney,
fill the stockings, distribute the remaining presents under the tree,
eat what ever snacks been that been left, get back up and move on to the
next house. By calculating the trip we'll find out that Sanat need to travel
at 650 miles per second, 3000 times the speed of sound that is....
the fastest man made vehicle on eart is Ulysses space probe, which does about
27.4 miles per second - a conventional reindeer can run top 15 miles per hour.

4. The payload on sleigh adds another interesting element. Assuming that eash
child only gets a normal lego.. (2 pounds), the sleigh is then carring
c 'arm'
321.300 tons, not counting Santa which is told be invariable described as an
overweight. On land a reindeer can pull about 300 pounds.... we need
214.200 reindeer unless the flying can carry at least more then 10 times their
cousin. This increases the payload again.. to 353.430 tons.

5. 353.000 tons traveling at 650 miles per second generates enormous energy,
like a space shuttle entering the atmosphere. The lead pair of reindeer
will absorb 14.3 QUINTILLION jouls of energy per second. In short the
sleigh will burst into almost instantenously, the entire reindeer team will be
vaporized within 4.26 thousandths of a second. Santa meanwhile will be subjected
to centrifugal forces of 17,500.06 times greater then gravity, will be pinned
to the back of his sleigh by 4,315,015 pounds of force.

IN CONCLUSION - if Santa ever DID deliver the presents on Christmas Eve

HE IS DEAD NOW.... Merry Christmas...

Greetings, Santa! On this week before the Night Before
Christmas, I felt it was appropriate to share with you this,
my last electronic piece of Kringle-related mail for the year
before you set off on the Great Journey. Santa, we are indeed
lucky that you are a part of all the lives of the children
of this Planet. Eleven years ago, through the actions of a
bunch of humans working out of England's famous Pinewood
Studios, I was permanently convinced about exactly how
vital and important your magic truly is. As the semi-legendary
PROBISC --- Professional Believer in Santa Claus --- I have
for the past decade made it my business to take Santa, his
life, deeds and works very seriously. We at Electric Pirates
and its Family of Companies have long ago adopted this
method of thinking to the point where we don't allow anyone
to speak any ill will about the ol' Kringlemeister. Simply
put, we love Santa. And we won't be timid about coming
to his defense. In closing, we want all of you to know
that long as children continue to reign in that ever-unchanging
Kingdom of the Imagination, there will always be a Santa Claus.
And let this be my personal guarantee: Electric Pirates and
its employees and their families will be right there, ready
to stand with Santa to defend and honor the true spirit of
Christmas. In that knowledge, I, Richard Washington,
Founder and Chairman of Electric Pirates Holdings, would
like to wish all of you a blessed and very magical Christmas,
and loads and loads of good health and merriment in the
coming New Year; and, indeed, in the coming Millenium.
In 1997, Santa's best and most loyal elves will be the ones
flying the ol' Jolly Roger --- because they'll be workin'
for us! Happy Holidays from the entire Electric Pirates
Family!
